Perf tip: Stop using babel-preset-es2015. It's deprecated.

Use babel-preset-env instead. The env preset only transpiles the features that your target browsers don't support.

Perf tip: Stop using babel-preset-es2015. It's deprecated.

Use babel-preset-env instead. The env preset only transpiles the features that your target browsers don't support.

Result? Smaller bundle.
